tracer.setStandby(camelContext.isBacklogTracingStandby());\n            tracer.setTraceTemplates(camelContext.isBacklogTracingTemplates());\n            tracer.setTraceRests(camelContext.isBacklogTracingRests());\n            camelContext.getCamelContextExtension().addContextPlugin(BacklogTracer.class, tracer);\n        }\n        return tracer;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @param  camelContext   the camel context from which the {@link BacklogDebugger} should be found.\n     * @param  createIfAbsent indicates whether a {@link BacklogDebugger} should createIfAbsent} is set to {@code true}, {@code null} otherwise.\n     */\n    private static BacklogDebugger getBacklogDebugger(CamelContext camelContext, boolean createIfAbsent) {\n                 match = PatternHelper.matchPattern(definition.getShortName(), pattern);\n                }\n                // location and line number\n                if (!match && pattern.contains(\":\")) {\n                    // try with line number and location\n                    String pnum = StringHelper.afterLast(pattern, \":\");\n                    if (pnum != null) 140→                    // it on the fly\n   141→                }\n   142→            }\n   143→        }\n   144→\n   145→        // configure message history\n   146→        if     internal.addRouteLifecycleAdvice(camelContext, route, definition);\n   328→\n   329→        // add advices\n   330→        if (definition.getRestBindingDefinition() != null) {\n   331→  463→                            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\n   464→                                    \"Cannot set route property \" + property + \" as it is a reserved property\");\n   465→                        }\n   466→                    }\n   467→                    routeProperties.put(key, val);\n   468→                } catch (Exception e) {\n   469→                    throw 477→     * Advice for moving message body into a variable when using variableReceive mode\n   478→     */\n   479→    private static class VariableAdvice implements 493→            exchange.getMessage().setBody(null);\n   494→            return body;\n   495→        }\n   496→\n   497→        @Override\n   498→        public void after(Exchange exchange, Object org.apache.camel.support.ExchangeHelper;\nimport org.apache.camel.support.LoggerHelper;\nimport org.apache.camel.support.PluginHelper;\nimport org.apache.camel.support.service.ServiceSupport;\nimport org.apache.camel.util.IOHelper;\nimport org.slf4j.Logger;\nimport org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;\n\npublic class RouteReifier extends ProcessorReifier<RouteDefinition> {\n\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(RouteReifier.class);\n\n    private static final String[] RESERVED_PROPERTIES = new String[] {\n            Route.ID_PROPERTY, Route.CUSTOM_ID_PROPERTY, Route.PARENT_PROPERTY,\n            Route.DESCRIPTION_PROPERTY, Route.NOTE_PROPERTY,\n            Route.GROUP_PROPERTY, Route.NODE_PREFIX_ID_PROPERTY,\n            Route.REST_PROPERTY, Route.CONFIGURATION_ID_PROPERTY };\n\n    public RouteReifier(CamelContext camelContext, ProcessorDefinition<?> definition) {\n        super(camelContext, (RouteDefinition) definition);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Processor createProcessor() throws Exception {\n        throw new UnsupportedOperationException(\"Not implemented for RouteDefinition\");\n    }\n\n    public Route createRoute() {\n        try {\n            return doCreateRoute();\n        } catch (FailedToCreateRouteException e) {\n            throw e;\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            // location on route is stored on input\n            ProcessorDefinitionHelper.prepareSourceLocation(definition.getResource(), definition.getInput());\n            String source = LoggerHelper.getSourceLocationOnly(definition.getInput());\n            throw new FailedToCreateRouteException(definition.getRouteId(), source, definition.toString(), e);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Implementation methods\n    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    protected Route doCreateRoute() throws Exception {\n        // resolve endpoint\n        Endpoint endpoint = definition.getInput().getEndpoint();\n        if (endpoint == null) {\n            EndpointConsumerResolver def = definition.getInput().getEndpointConsumerBuilder();\n            if (def != null) {\n                endpoint = def.resolve(camelContext);\n            } else {\n                endpoint = resolveEndpoint(definition.getInput().getEndpointUri());\n            }\n        }\n\n        // create route\n        String id = definition.idOrCreate(camelContext.getCamelContextExtension().getContextPlugin(NodeIdFactory.class));\n        String desc = definition.getDescriptionText();\n        String note = definition.getNote();\n\n        Route route = PluginHelper.getRouteFactory(camelContext).createRoute(camelContext, definition, id,\n                desc, note, endpoint, definition.getResource());\n\n        // configure error handler\n        route.setErrorHandlerFactory(definition.getErrorHandlerFactory());\n\n        // configure variable\n        String variable = parseString(definition.getInput().getVariableReceive());\n        if (variable != null) {\n            // when using variable we need to turn on original message\n            route.setAllowUseOriginalMessage(true);\n        }\n\n        // configure tracing\n        if (definition.getTrace() != null) {\n            Boolean isTrace = parseBoolean(definition.getTrace());\n            if (isTrace != null) {\n                route.setTracing(isTrace);\n                if (isTrace) {\n                    LOG.debug(\"Tracing is enabled on route: {}\", definition.getId());\n                    // tracing is added in the DefaultChannel so we can enable\n                    // it on the fly\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // configure message history\n        if (definition.getMessageHistory() != null) {\n            Boolean isMessageHistory = parseBoolean(definition.getMessageHistory());\n            if (isMessageHistory != null) {\n                route.setMessageHistory(isMessageHistory);\n                if (isMessageHistory) {\n                    LOG.debug(\"Message history is enabled on route: {}\", definition.getId());\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // configure Log EIP mask\n        if (definition.getLogMask() != null) {\n            Boolean isLogMask = parseBoolean(definition.getLogMask());\n            if (isLogMask != null) {\n                route.setLogMask(isLogMask);\n                if (isLogMask) {\n                    LOG.debug(\"Security mask for Logging is enabled on route: {}\", definition.getId());\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // configure stream caching\n        if (definition.getStreamCache() != null) {\n            Boolean isStreamCache = parseBoolean(definition.getStreamCache());\n            if (isStreamCache != null) {\n                route.setStreamCaching(isStreamCache);\n                if (isStreamCache) {\n                    LOG.debug(\"StreamCaching is enabled on route: {}\", definition.getId());\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // configure delayer\n        if (definition.getDelayer() != null) {\n            Long delayer = parseDuration(definition.getDelayer());\n            if (delayer != null) {\n                route.setDelayer(delayer);\n                if (delayer > 0) {\n                    LOG.debug(\"Delayer is enabled with: {} ms. on route: {}\", delayer, definition.getId());\n                } else {\n                    LOG.debug(\"Delayer is disabled on route: {}\", definition.getId());\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        // configure auto startup\n        Boolean isAutoStartup = parseBoolean(definition.getAutoStartup());\n\n        // configure startup order\n        Integer startupOrder = definition.getStartupOrder();\n\n        // configure shutdown\n        if (definition.getShutdownRoute() != null) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Using ShutdownRoute {} on route: {}\", definition.getShutdownRoute(), definition.getId());\n            route.setShutdownRoute(parse(ShutdownRoute.class, definition.getShutdownRoute()));\n        }\n        if (definition.getShutdownRunningTask() != null) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Using ShutdownRunningTask {} on route: {}\", definition.getShutdownRunningTask(), definition.getId());\n            route.setShutdownRunningTask(parse(ShutdownRunningTask.class, definition.getShutdownRunningTask()));\n        }\n\n        // should inherit the intercept strategies we have defined\n        route.getInterceptStrategies().addAll(definition.getInterceptStrategies());\n\n        // notify route context created\n        for (LifecycleStrategy strategy : camelContext.getLifecycleStrategies()) {\n            strategy.onRouteContextCreate(route);\n        }\n\n        // validate route has output processors\n        if (!hasOutputs(definition.getOutputs(), true)) {\n            String at = definition.getInput().toString();\n            Exception cause = new IllegalArgumentException(\n                    \"Route \" + definition.getId() + \" has no output processors.\"\n                                                           + \" You need to add outputs to the route such as to(\\\"log:foo\\\").\");\n            // location on route is stored on input\n            ProcessorDefinitionHelper.prepareSourceLocation(definition.getResource(), definition.getInput());\n            String source = LoggerHelper.getSourceLocationOnly(definition.getInput());\n            throw new FailedToCreateRouteException(\n                    definition.getRouteId(), source, definition.toString(), at, cause);\n        }\n\n        List<ProcessorDefinition<?>> list = new ArrayList<>(definition.getOutputs());\n        for (ProcessorDefinition<?> output : list) {\n            try {\n                ProcessorReifier<?> reifier = ProcessorReifier.reifier(route, output);\n\n                // ensure node has id assigned\n                String outputId\n                        = output.idOrCreate(camelContext.getCamelContextExtension().getContextPlugin(NodeIdFactory.class));\n                String eip = reifier.getClass().getSimpleName().replace(\"Reifier\", \"\");\n                StartupStep step = camelContext.getCamelContextExtension().getStartupStepRecorder()\n                        .beginStep(ProcessorReifier.class, outputId, \"Create \" + eip + \" Processor\");\n\n                reifier.addRoutes();\n\n                camelContext.getCamelContextExtension().getStartupStepRecorder().endStep(step);\n            } catch (Exception e) {\n                // location on route is stored on input\n                String source = LoggerHelper\n                        .getLineNumberLoggerName(definition.getInput() != null ? definition.getInput().getLocation() : null);\n                throw new FailedToCreateRouteException(\n                        definition.getRouteId(), source, definition.toString(), output.toString(), e);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // now lets turn all the event driven consumer processors into a single route\n        List<Processor> eventDrivenProcessors = route.getEventDrivenProcessors();\n        if (eventDrivenProcessors.isEmpty()) {\n            return null;\n        }\n\n        // Set route properties\n        Map<String, Object> routeProperties = computeRouteProperties();\n\n        // always use a pipeline even if there are only 1 processor as the pipeline\n        // handles preparing the response from the exchange in regard to IN vs OUT messages etc\n        RoutePipeline target = new RoutePipeline(camelContext, eventDrivenProcessors);\n        target.setRouteId(id);\n\n        // and wrap it in a unit of work so the UoW is on the top, so the entire route will be in the same UoW\n        InternalProcessor internal = PluginHelper.getInternalProcessorFactory(camelContext)\n                .addUnitOfWorkProcessorAdvice(camelContext, target, route);\n\n        // configure route policy\n        if (definition.getRoutePolicies() != null && !definition.getRoutePolicies().isEmpty()) {\n            for (RoutePolicy policy : definition.getRoutePolicies()) {\n                LOG.debug(\"RoutePolicy is enabled: {} on route: {}\", policy, definition.getId());\n                route.getRoutePolicyList().add(policy);\n            }\n        }\n        if (definition.getRoutePolicyRef() != null) {\n            StringTokenizer policyTokens = new StringTokenizer(definition.getRoutePolicyRef(), \",\");\n            while (policyTokens.hasMoreTokens()) {\n                String ref = policyTokens.nextToken().trim();\n                RoutePolicy policy = mandatoryLookup(ref, RoutePolicy.class);\n                LOG.debug(\"RoutePolicy is enabled: {} on route: {}\", policy, definition.getId());\n                route.getRoutePolicyList().add(policy);\n            }\n        }\n        if (camelContext.getRoutePolicyFactories() != null) {\n            for (RoutePolicyFactory factory : camelContext.getRoutePolicyFactories()) {\n                RoutePolicy policy = factory.createRoutePolicy(camelContext, definition.getId(), definition);\n                if (policy != null) {\n                    LOG.debug(\"RoutePolicy is enabled: {} on route: {}\", policy, definition.getId());\n                    route.getRoutePolicyList().add(policy);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        // and then optionally add route policy processor if a custom policy is set\n        List<RoutePolicy> routePolicyList = route.getRoutePolicyList();\n        if (routePolicyList != null && !routePolicyList.isEmpty()) {\n            for (RoutePolicy policy : routePolicyList) {\n                // add policy as service if we have not already done that (eg possible if two routes have the same service)\n                // this ensures Camel can control the lifecycle of the policy\n                if (!camelContext.hasService(policy)) {\n                    try {\n                        // inject route\n                        if (policy instanceof RouteAware ra) {\n                            ra.setRoute(route);\n                        }\n                        camelContext.addService(policy);\n                    } catch (Exception e) {\n                        throw RuntimeCamelException.wrapRuntimeCamelException(e);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n\n            internal.addRoutePolicyAdvice(routePolicyList);\n        }\n\n        // wrap in route inflight processor to track number of inflight exchanges for the route\n        internal.addRouteInflightRepositoryAdvice(camelContext.getInflightRepository(), route.getRouteId());\n\n        // wrap in JMX instrumentation processor that is used for performance stats\n        ManagementInterceptStrategy managementInterceptStrategy = route.getManagementInterceptStrategy();\n        if (managementInterceptStrategy != null) {\n            internal.addManagementInterceptStrategy(managementInterceptStrategy.createProcessor(\"route\"));\n        }\n\n        // wrap in route lifecycle\n        internal.addRouteLifecycleAdvice(camelContext, route, definition);\n\n        // add advices\n        if (definition.getRestBindingDefinition() != null) {\n            try {\n                // when disabling bean or processor we should also disable rest-dsl binding advice\n                boolean disabled\n                        = \"true\".equalsIgnoreCase(route.getCamelContext().getGlobalOption(DISABLE_BEAN_OR_PROCESS_PROCESSORS));\n                if (!disabled) {\n                    internal.addAdvice(\n                            new RestBindingReifier(route, definition.getRestBindingDefinition()).createRestBindingAdvice());\n                }\n            } catch (Exception e) {\n                throw RuntimeCamelException.wrapRuntimeCamelException(e);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // wrap in contract\n        if (definition.getInputType() != null || definition.getOutputType() != null) {\n            Contract contract = new Contract();\n            if (definition.getInputType() != null) {\n                contract.setInputType(parseString(definition.getInputType().getUrn()));\n                contract.setValidateInput(parseBoolean(definition.getInputType().getValidate(), false));\n            }\n            if (definition.getOutputType() != null) {\n                contract.setOutputType(parseString(definition.getOutputType().getUrn()));\n                contract.setValidateOutput(parseBoolean(definition.getOutputType().getValidate(), false));\n            }\n            internal.addAdvice(new ContractAdvice(contract));\n            // make sure to enable data type as its in use when using\n            // input/output types on routes\n            camelContext.setUseDataType(true);\n        }\n\n        // wrap with variable\n        if (variable != null) {\n            internal.addAdvice(new VariableAdvice(variable));\n        }\n\n        // and create the route that wraps all of this\n        route.setProcessor(internal);\n        route.getProperties().putAll(routeProperties);\n        route.setStartupOrder(startupOrder);\n        if (isAutoStartup != null) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Using AutoStartup {} on route: {}\", isAutoStartup, definition.getId());\n            route.setAutoStartup(isAutoStartup);\n        }\n\n        // after the route is created then set the route on the policy processor(s) so we get hold of it\n        internal.setRouteOnAdvices(route);\n\n        // invoke init on route policy\n        if (routePolicyList != null && !routePolicyList.isEmpty()) {\n            for (RoutePolicy policy : routePolicyList) {\n                policy.onInit(route);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // inject the route error handler for processors that are error handler aware\n        // this needs to be done here at the end because the route may be transactional and have a transaction error handler\n        // automatic be configured which some EIPs like Multicast/RecipientList needs to be using for special fine-grained error handling\n        ErrorHandlerFactory builder = route.getErrorHandlerFactory();\n        Processor errorHandler = ((ModelCamelContext) camelContext).getModelReifierFactory().createErrorHandler(route,\n                builder, null);\n        prepareErrorHandlerAware(route, errorHandler);\n\n        // only during startup phase\n        if (camelContext.getStatus().ordinal() < ServiceStatus.Started.ordinal()) {\n            // okay route has been created from the model, then the model is no longer needed, and we can de-reference\n            camelContext.getCamelContextExtension().addBootstrap(route::clearRouteModel);\n        }\n\n        if (definition.getRouteTemplateContext() != null) {\n            // make route stop beans from the local repository (route templates / kamelets)\n            Service wrapper = new ServiceSupport() {\n                @Override\n                protected void doStop() throws Exception {\n                    close();\n                }\n\n                @Override\n                public void close() throws IOException {\n                    BeanRepository repo = definition.getRouteTemplateContext().getLocalBeanRepository();\n                    if (repo instanceof Closeable obj) {\n                        IOHelper.close(obj);\n                    }\n                    super.close();\n                }\n            };\n            route.addService(wrapper, true);\n        }\n\n        return route;\n    }\n\n    private void prepareErrorHandlerAware(Route route, Processor errorHandler) {\n        List<Processor> processors = route.filter(\"*\");\n        for (Processor p : processors) {\n            if (p instanceof ErrorHandlerAware errorHandlerAware) {\n                errorHandlerAware.setErrorHandler(errorHandler);\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    protected Map<String, Object> computeRouteProperties() {\n        Map<String, Object> routeProperties = new HashMap<>();\n        routeProperties.put(Route.ID_PROPERTY, definition.getId());\n        routeProperties.put(Route.CUSTOM_ID_PROPERTY, Boolean.toString(definition.hasCustomIdAssigned()));\n        routeProperties.put(Route.PARENT_PROPERTY, Integer.toHexString(definition.hashCode()));\n        routeProperties.put(Route.DESCRIPTION_PROPERTY, definition.getDescriptionText());\n        routeProperties.put(Route.NOTE_PROPERTY, definition.getNote());\n        if (definition.getGroup() != null) {\n            routeProperties.put(Route.GROUP_PROPERTY, definition.getGroup());\n        }\n        if (definition.getNodePrefixId() != null) {\n            routeProperties.put(Route.NODE_PREFIX_ID_PROPERTY, definition.getNodePrefixId());\n        }\n        String rest = Boolean.toString(definition.isRest() != null && definition.isRest());\n        routeProperties.put(Route.REST_PROPERTY, rest);\n        String template = Boolean.toString(definition.isTemplate() != null && definition.isTemplate());\n        routeProperties.put(Route.TEMPLATE_PROPERTY, template);\n        String kamelet = Boolean.toString(definition.isKamelet() != null && definition.isKamelet());\n        routeProperties.put(Route.KAMELET_PROPERTY, kamelet);\n        if (definition.getAppliedRouteConfigurationIds() != null) {\n            routeProperties.put(Route.CONFIGURATION_ID_PROPERTY,\n                    String.join(\",\", definition.getAppliedRouteConfigurationIds()));\n        }\n\n        List<PropertyDefinition> properties = definition.getRouteProperties();\n        if (properties != null) {\n            for (PropertyDefinition prop : properties) {\n                try {\n                    final String key = parseString(prop.getKey());\n                    final String val = parseString(prop.getValue());\n                    for (String property : RESERVED_PROPERTIES) {\n                        if (property.equalsIgnoreCase(key)) {\n                            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\n                                    \"Cannot set route property \" + property + \" as it is a reserved property\");\n                        }\n                    }\n                    routeProperties.put(key, val);\n                } catch (Exception e) {\n                    throw RuntimeCamelException.wrapRuntimeCamelException(e);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        return routeProperties;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Advice for moving message body into a variable when using variableReceive mode\n     */\n    private static class VariableAdvice implements CamelInternalProcessorAdvice<Object> {\n\n        private final String name;\n\n        public VariableAdvice(String name) {\n            this.name = name;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public Object before(Exchange exchange) throws Exception {\n            // move body to variable\n            ExchangeHelper.setVariableFromMessageBodyAndHeaders(exchange, name, exchange.getMessage());\n            // remember body\n            Object body = exchange.getMessage().getBody();\n            exchange.getMessage().setBody(null);\n            return body;\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public void after(Exchange exchange, Object data) throws Exception {\n            // restore body if body has not been changed\n            if (data != null && exchange.getMessage().getBody() == null) {\n                exchange.getMessage().setBody(data);\n            }\n        }\n\n    }\n\n}\n","numLines":508,"startLine":1,"totalLines":508}}}

`ProcessorReifier.java:834` → `makeProcessor()`\n   — Calls `createProcessor()` (abstract, implemented by each EIP reifier) to instantiate the concrete `Processor` (e.g., `SendProcessor`, node history.\n   — Wraps `nextProcessor` in each `InterceptStrategy` (decorating in reverse order for correct invocation sequence).\n   — Sets the final wrapped output on `this.output`.\n\n7. **Error handler wrapping**: `ProcessorReifier.java:721` → `wrapChannelInErrorHandler(channel, inheritErrorHandler)`\n   — Creates an error handler around `channel.getOutput()` and sets it as `channel.errorHandler`.\n   — `channel.getOutput()` returns `errorHandler != null ? errorHandler : output`.\n\n8. **Route pipeline assembly**: `RouteReifier.java:263`\n   — All event-driven processors (channels) from `route.getEventDrivenProcessors()` are assembled into:\n     `RoutePipeline target = new RoutePipeline(camelContext, eventDrivenProcessors)`\n\n9. **UoW wrapping**: `RouteReifier.java:267`\n   — `InternalProcessorFactory.addUnitOfWorkProcessorAdvice(camelContext, target, route)` returns a `CamelInternalProcessor` that manages `UnitOfWork` lifecycle for the whole exchange.\n\n10. **Additional advices**: `RouteReifier.java:314–376`\n    — Route policy, inflight repository, JMX instrumentation, route lifecycle, REST binding, contract validation, variable `CamelInternalProcessor` becomes the route's root processor.\n\n### Startup Time: Consumer Wiring\n\n12. **RouteService.doSetup()**: `RouteService.java:161`\n    — Calls `route.initializeServices()` which calls `DefaultRoute.gatherRootServices()`.\n\n13. **Consumer creation**: `DefaultRoute.java:685`\n    — `consumer = endpoint.createConsumer(processor)` — passes the route's `CamelInternalProcessor` as the `Processor` argument to the endpoint's consumer factory method.\n    — The `Consumer` (e.g., a timer thread, JMS listener, HTTP server) now holds a reference to the entire processing chain.\n\n### Runtime: Message Flow\n\n14. **Consumer receives message** → creates `Exchange` via `createExchange(autoRelease)` → calls `asyncProcessor.process(exchange, callback)`.\n\n15. **CamelInternalProcessor.process()** → runs `before()` on all advices (UoW init, route policy, JMX) → delegates to `RoutePipeline`.\n\n16. **RoutePipeline** → iterates its `List<AsyncProcessor>` (the `DefaultChannel` instances) via `PipelineTask.run()` in the `ReactiveExecutor`.\n\n17. **DefaultChannel** (also a `CamelInternalProcessor`) → runs node-level advices (tracing, debugging, message history) → delegates to `errorHandler` (which in turn delegates to `output` = the interceptor-wrapped `nextProcessor`).\n\n18. **nextProcessor** → the concrete EIP implementation (e.g., `SendProcessor`, `FilterProcessor`, `SetBodyProcessor`).\n\n19. **SendProcessor** → acquires `AsyncProducer` from `ProducerCache` → calls `producer.process(exchange, callback)` → sends to destination `Endpoint`.\n\n20. **Pipeline continuation**: after each step's `AsyncCallback.done()` fires, `PipelineTask.run()` is re-scheduled by `ReactiveExecutor` to process the next processor in the list.\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Design Patterns Identified\n\n**1. Pipes-and-Filters (EIP)**\nThe `Pipeline` / `RoutePipeline` class is the canonical implementation of the Pipes-and-Filters integration pattern. Each `ProcessorDefinition` in the DSL becomes a filter step; the `DefaultChannel` between adjacent steps is the pipe. The `PipelineTask` inner class manages the sequential iteration asynchronously via `ReactiveExecutor.scheduleMain()`.\n\n**2. Message Endpoint (EIP)**\nThe `Endpoint` interface is a direct implementation of the Message Endpoint pattern. It decouples routing logic from transport details: the same `Processor` chain is connected to any technology (HTTP, JMS, file, etc.) simply by passing it to `endpoint.createConsumer(processor)`.\n\n**3. Event-Driven Consumer (EIP)**\n`DefaultConsumer` and its subclasses implement Event-Driven Consumers. Once started, they passively receive messages and forward them to the pipeline by calling `processor.process(exchange, callback)`.\n\n**4. Decorator / Advice (GoF)**\n`CamelInternalProcessor` is a decorator that uses an advice chain (`List<CamelInternalProcessorAdvice<?>>`) rather than a stack of wrappers. Each advice implements `before(exchange)` / `after(exchange, state)`. This AOP-like model reduces stack depth and makes the advice list inspectable at runtime. `DefaultChannel` inherits this pattern for node-level cross-cutting concerns.\n\n**5. Template Method (GoF)**\n`ProcessorReifier` uses Template Method: `makeProcessor()` is the template calling `createProcessor()` (abstract, implemented by each concrete reifier), then `wrapProcessor()`. `wrapChannel()` always follows the same steps (create channel → add interceptors → init channel → wrap in error handler → post-init).\n\n**6. Strategy (GoF)**\n`InterceptStrategy` is a Strategy pattern applied at channel initialization. Multiple strategies are composed in order. `ErrorHandlerFactory` is similarly a Strategy for creating error handlers.\n\n**7. Factory Method (GoF)**\n`Component.createEndpoint()` is a Factory Method. `ProcessorReifier.reifier()` uses a dispatch table (`coreReifier()` + `PROCESSORS` custom map) as an extensible factory registry, following Open/Closed principle.\n\n**8. Command (GoF)**\n`Exchange` is a Command object: it carries all message data, headers, properties, and the eventual callback through the entire pipeline without coupling sender and receiver.\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility |\n|-----------|---------------|\n| `Component` | URI-to-Endpoint factory; technology adapter entry point |\n| `Endpoint` | Exchange factory; Consumer and Producer factory; technology configuration |\n| `Consumer` | Transport-layer listener; creates Exchanges and drives the pipeline |\n| `Channel` (DefaultChannel) | Inter-node pipe; intercept point for cross-cutting (tracing, JMX, debug, error handling) |\n| `Pipeline` / `RoutePipeline` | Sequential chaining of Channel processors; async scheduling via ReactiveExecutor |\n| `CamelInternalProcessor` | AOP advice executor; UoW management, route policies, inflight tracking at route and node level |\n| `ProcessorReifier` | Build-time adapter: translates `ProcessorDefinition` model nodes to runtime `Processor`+`Channel` instances |\n| `RouteReifier` | Build-time orchestrator: resolves endpoint, drives EIP reification, assembles RoutePipeline, wraps in UoW |\n| `RouteService` | Runtime lifecycle manager for a single route (setup, warm-up, start, stop, shutdown) |\n| `RouteDefinition` | Immutable DSL model representing a route's topology |\n| `SendProcessor` | Produces an outbound message to a destination Endpoint via ProducerCache |\n\n### Data Flow Description\n\n```\nDSL Definition (RouteDefinition)\n       ↓ RouteReifier.doCreateRoute()\nEndpoint resolved from URI\n       ↓ ProcessorReifier.reifier(route, eipNode).addRoutes() [per output EIP]\n         ↓ makeProcessor() → createProcessor() [concrete EIP Processor]\n         ↓ wrapChannel() → DefaultChannel.initChannel()\n              [interceptors layered: InterceptStrategy wrapping in reverse order]\n              [advices added: tracer, debugger, message history, node history]\n         ↓ wrapChannelInErrorHandler() [ErrorHandler wraps channel output]\n         channel → route.getEventDrivenProcessors()\n       ↓ RoutePipeline(eventDrivenProcessors)\n       ↓ CamelInternalProcessor wrapping RoutePipeline [UoW, policies, JMX]\n       ↓ route.setProcessor(internal)\n       ↓ endpoint.createConsumer(processor) → Consumer holds full chain\n\nRUNTIME:\nConsumer.receives() → Exchange created\n  → CamelInternalProcessor [UoW begin, policy onExchangeBegin, JMX]\n    → RoutePipeline [PipelineTask iterates via ReactiveExecutor]\n      → DefaultChannel₁ [advices: trace/debug/history; error handler wraps]\n        → EIP Processor₁ (SetBody, Filter, etc.)\n      → DefaultChannel₂ [advices; error handler wraps]\n        → EIP Processor₂ (SendProcessor)\n          → ProducerCache → AsyncProducer.process()\n            → Endpoint₂.producer sends message\n  ← AsyncCallback chain unwinds back through Pipeline\n  ← CamelInternalProcessor [UoW complete, policy onExchangeDone, JMX]\nConsumer.releaseExchange()\n```\n\n### Interface Contracts Between Components\n\n- **Component → Endpoint**: `Component.createEndpoint(uri)` produces an `Endpoint`; the component owns URI parsing and endpoint configuration.\n- **Endpoint → Consumer**: `Endpoint.createConsumer(Processor)` injects the route's pipeline as the downstream handler; transport details stay encapsulated in the Consumer.\n- **Endpoint → Producer**: `Endpoint.createProducer()` produces a `Producer`; `SendProcessor` uses `ProducerCache` to pool and reuse producers.\n- **Channel contract**: `Channel.initChannel(route, definition, child, interceptors, nextProcessor, routeDef, first)` is called exactly once at build time; `postInitChannel()` finalizes JMX instrumentation after error handler is known.\n- **Pipeline contract**: `Pipeline` expects each step to be an `AsyncProcessor`; it manages continuations via `AsyncCallback.done(doneSync)` and `ReactiveExecutor.schedule()`.\n- **CamelInternalProcessorAdvice contract**: `before(exchange)` returns state object; `after(exchange, state)` receives it back; `hasState()` controls pooling behavior.\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nApache Camel routes a message by first translating the DSL model (`RouteDefinition` with its `ProcessorDefinition` tree) into a runtime graph at startup via `RouteReifier`: each EIP node becomes a concrete `Processor` wrapped in a `DefaultChannel` (which layers interceptors, tracing, debugging, and error handling via the AOP-style `CamelInternalProcessorAdvice` mechanism), and the ordered sequence of channels is collected into a `RoutePipeline`. The entire pipeline is then wrapped in a root `CamelInternalProcessor` that manages `UnitOfWork` and route-level cross-cutting concerns, and this processor is passed to `Endpoint.createConsumer()` so the transport-specific `Consumer` drives the pipeline when messages arrive. At runtime, messages flow as `Exchange` objects through `CamelInternalProcessor` → `RoutePipeline` → `DefaultChannel₁` → `EIPProcessor₁` → ... → `DefaultChannel_N` → `SendProcessor` → destination `Producer`, with asynchronous continuations scheduled by the `ReactiveExecutor` and each channel providing an interception boundary for error handling, management, and observability.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":212,"cache_read_input_tokens":77639,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":212,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":18,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"05c58a47-d0ba-4b4a-a932-0a811199a3d0","uuid":"69ced2ec-a246-4cbd-97c4-be68e3d054b5"}

references inbound `Consumer`, route `Processor` (the pipeline), and its originating `Endpoint`\n\n### Base Implementations (`core/camel-support`)\n- `core/camel-support/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/support/DefaultComponent.java` — base `Component` implementation; resolves destination `Endpoint`, sends via `ProducerCache`\n\n### Runtime Engine (`core/camel-base-engine`)\n- `core/camel-base-engine/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/impl/engine/DefaultChannel.java` — implements `Channel`; extends `CamelInternalProcessor`; wires in interceptors (tracing, debugging, stream caching, JMX instrumentation) and error handlers around the next `Processor`\n- `core/camel-base-engine/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/impl/engine/CamelInternalProcessor.java` — AOP-style advice executor; runs ordered `CamelInternalProcessorAdvice` before/after the delegate processor (UoW, route policy, JMX, tracing, debugging, message history)\n- `core/camel-base-engine/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/impl/engine/DefaultRoute.java` — runtime `Route` implementation; stores `Consumer`, `Processor` (InternalProcessor wrapping RoutePipeline), `Endpoint`; `gatherRootServices()` calls `endpoint.createConsumer(processor)` to wire consumer to pipeline\n- `core/camel-base-engine/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/impl/engine/RouteService.java` — manages route lifecycle; `doSetup()` initializes endpoint and services; `doWarmUp()` starts endpoint and registers route; `doStart()` starts the route and invokes route policies\n- `core/camel-base-engine/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/impl/engine/AbstractCamelContext.java` — central context; delegates route startup to `InternalRouteStartupManager`\n\n### DSL Model (`core/camel-core-model`)\n- `core/camel-core-model/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/model/RouteDefinition.java` — DSL model node for a route; tree structure with parent/child relationships\n\n### Reifiers (`core/camel-core-reifier`)\n- `core/camel-core-reifier/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/reifier/RouteReifier.java` — **model-to-runtime bridge**; converts `RouteDefinition` → runtime `Route`; resolves endpoint, calls `ProcessorReifier.reifier(route, output).addRoutes()` for each output, assembles `RoutePipeline`, wraps in `CamelInternalProcessor` with UoW advice\n- `core/camel-core-reifier/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/reifier/ProcessorReifier.java` — abstract base reifier; `makeProcessor()` creates processor and wraps it in a `Channel`; `wrapChannel()` instantiates `DefaultChannel`, adds `InterceptStrategy` list, optionally adds error handler; `addRoutes()` adds the wrapped channel to `route.getEventDrivenProcessors()`\n- `core/camel-core-reifier/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/reifier/PipelineReifier.java` — creates nested `Pipeline` for explicit `<pipeline>` DSL nodes\n\n---\n\n## Dependency Chain\n\n### Build Time: DSL Model → Runtime Route\n\n1. **Entry point**: `core/camel-core-model/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/model/RouteDefinition.java`\n   — DSL builder methods (Java/YAML/XML) accumulate `ProcessorDefinition<?>` nodes into `getOutputs()`.\n\n2. **Reification trigger**: `core/camel-core-reifier/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/reifier/RouteReifier.java:87` → `doCreateRoute()`\n   — Called by `CamelContext` during startup. Resolves the `from(...)` URI to an `Endpoint`.\n\n3. **Per-EIP reifier dispatch**: `ProcessorReifier.java:231` → `ProcessorReifier.reifier(route, output).addRoutes()`\n   — Iterates `RouteDefinition.getOutputs()` and dispatches each `ProcessorDefinition` to its specific reifier via `coreReifier()` (pattern-match on class type).\n\n4. **Processor creation**: `ProcessorReifier.java:834` → `makeProcessor()`\n   — Calls `createProcessor()` (abstract, implemented by each EIP reifier) to instantiate the concrete `Processor` (e.g., `SendProcessor`, `FilterProcessor`, `Pipeline`).\n\n5. **Channel wiring**: `ProcessorReifier.java:650` → `wrapChannel(processor, child)`\n   — Creates a `DefaultChannel` via `InternalProcessorFactory.createChannel()`.\n   — Collects `InterceptStrategy` list from CamelContext + Route + definition.\n   — Calls `channel.initChannel(route, definition, child, interceptors, processor, routeDefinition, first)`.\n\n6. **Channel initialization**: `DefaultChannel.java:149` → `initChannel(...)`\n   — Adds advices for debugger, backlog tracer, logger tracer, message history, node history.\n   — Wraps `nextProcessor` in each `InterceptStrategy` (decorating in reverse order for correct invocation sequence).\n   — Sets the final wrapped output on `this.output`.\n\n7. **Error handler wrapping**: `ProcessorReifier.java:721` → `wrapChannelInErrorHandler(channel, inheritErrorHandler)`\n   — Creates an error handler around `channel.getOutput()` and sets it as `channel.errorHandler`.\n   — `channel.getOutput()` returns `errorHandler != null ? errorHandler : output`.\n\n8. **Route pipeline assembly**: `RouteReifier.java:263`\n   — All event-driven processors (channels) from `route.getEventDrivenProcessors()` are assembled into:\n     `RoutePipeline target = new RoutePipeline(camelContext, eventDrivenProcessors)`\n\n9. **UoW wrapping**: `RouteReifier.java:267`\n   — `InternalProcessorFactory.addUnitOfWorkProcessorAdvice(camelContext, target, route)` returns a `CamelInternalProcessor` that manages `UnitOfWork` lifecycle for the whole exchange.\n\n10. **Additional advices**: `RouteReifier.java:314–376`\n    — Route policy, inflight repository, JMX instrumentation, route lifecycle, REST binding, contract validation, variable handling advices are added to the root `CamelInternalProcessor`.\n\n11. **Route finalization**: `RouteReifier.java:367` → `route.setProcessor(internal)`\n    — The fully decorated `CamelInternalProcessor` becomes the route's root processor.\n\n### Startup Time: Consumer Wiring\n\n12. **RouteService.doSetup()**: `RouteService.java:161`\n    — Calls `route.initializeServices()` which calls `DefaultRoute.gatherRootServices()`.\n\n13. **Consumer creation**: `DefaultRoute.java:685`\n    — `consumer = endpoint.createConsumer(processor)` — passes the route's `CamelInternalProcessor` as the `Processor` argument to the endpoint's consumer factory method.\n    — The `Consumer` (e.g., a timer thread, JMS listener, HTTP server) now holds a reference to the entire processing chain.\n\n### Runtime: Message Flow\n\n14. **Consumer receives message** → creates `Exchange` via `createExchange(autoRelease)` → calls `asyncProcessor.process(exchange, callback)`.\n\n15. **CamelInternalProcessor.process()** → runs `before()` on all advices (UoW init, route policy, JMX) → delegates to `RoutePipeline`.\n\n16. **RoutePipeline** → iterates its `List<AsyncProcessor>` (the `DefaultChannel` instances) via `PipelineTask.run()` in the `ReactiveExecutor`.\n\n17. **DefaultChannel** (also a `CamelInternalProcessor`) → runs node-level advices (tracing, debugging, message history) → delegates to `errorHandler` (which in turn delegates to `output` = the interceptor-wrapped `nextProcessor`).\n\n18. **nextProcessor** → the concrete EIP implementation (e.g., `SendProcessor`, `FilterProcessor`, `SetBodyProcessor`).\n\n19. **SendProcessor** → acquires `AsyncProducer` from `ProducerCache` → calls `producer.process(exchange, callback)` → sends to destination `Endpoint`.\n\n20. **Pipeline continuation**: after each step's `AsyncCallback.done()` fires, `PipelineTask.run()` is re-scheduled by `ReactiveExecutor` to process the next processor in the list.\n\n---\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Design Patterns Identified\n\n**1. Pipes-and-Filters (EIP)**\nThe `Pipeline` / `RoutePipeline` class is the canonical implementation of the Pipes-and-Filters integration pattern. Each `ProcessorDefinition` in the DSL becomes a filter step; the `DefaultChannel` between adjacent steps is the pipe. The `PipelineTask` inner class manages the sequential iteration asynchronously via `ReactiveExecutor.scheduleMain()`.\n\n**2. Message Endpoint (EIP)**\nThe `Endpoint` interface is a direct implementation of the Message Endpoint pattern. It decouples routing logic from transport details: the same `Processor` chain is connected to any technology (HTTP, JMS, file, etc.) simply by passing it to `endpoint.createConsumer(processor)`.\n\n**3. Event-Driven Consumer (EIP)**\n`DefaultConsumer` and its subclasses implement Event-Driven Consumers. Once started, they passively receive messages and forward them to the pipeline by calling `processor.process(exchange, callback)`.\n\n**4. Decorator / Advice (GoF)**\n`CamelInternalProcessor` is a decorator that uses an advice chain (`List<CamelInternalProcessorAdvice<?>>`) rather than a stack of wrappers. Each advice implements `before(exchange)` / `after(exchange, state)`. This AOP-like model reduces stack depth and makes the advice list inspectable at runtime. `DefaultChannel` inherits this pattern for node-level cross-cutting concerns.\n\n**5. Template Method (GoF)**\n`ProcessorReifier` uses Template Method: `makeProcessor()` is the template calling `createProcessor()` (abstract, implemented by each concrete reifier), then `wrapProcessor()`. `wrapChannel()` always follows the same steps (create channel → add interceptors → init channel → wrap in error handler → post-init).\n\n**6. Strategy (GoF)**\n`InterceptStrategy` is a Strategy pattern applied at channel initialization. Multiple strategies are composed in order. `ErrorHandlerFactory` is similarly a Strategy for creating error handlers.\n\n**7. Factory Method (GoF)**\n`Component.createEndpoint()` is a Factory Method. `ProcessorReifier.reifier()` uses a dispatch table (`coreReifier()` + `PROCESSORS` custom map) as an extensible factory registry, following Open/Closed principle.\n\n**8. Command (GoF)**\n`Exchange` is a Command object: it carries all message data, headers, properties, and the eventual callback through the entire pipeline without coupling sender and receiver.\n\n### Component Responsibilities\n\n| Component | Responsibility |\n|-----------|---------------|\n| `Component` | URI-to-Endpoint factory; technology adapter entry point |\n| `Endpoint` | Exchange factory; Consumer and Producer factory; technology configuration |\n| `Consumer` | Transport-layer listener; creates Exchanges and drives the pipeline |\n| `Channel` (DefaultChannel) | Inter-node pipe; intercept point for cross-cutting (tracing, JMX, debug, error handling) |\n| `Pipeline` / `RoutePipeline` | Sequential chaining of Channel processors; async scheduling via ReactiveExecutor |\n| `CamelInternalProcessor` | AOP advice executor; UoW management, route policies, inflight tracking at route and node level |\n| `ProcessorReifier` | Build-time adapter: translates `ProcessorDefinition` model nodes to runtime `Processor`+`Channel` instances |\n| `RouteReifier` | Build-time orchestrator: resolves endpoint, drives EIP reification, assembles RoutePipeline, wraps in UoW |\n| `RouteService` | Runtime lifecycle manager for a single route (setup, warm-up, start, stop, shutdown) |\n| `RouteDefinition` | Immutable DSL model representing a route's topology |\n| `SendProcessor` | Produces an outbound message to a destination Endpoint via ProducerCache |\n\n### Data Flow Description\n\n```\nDSL Definition (RouteDefinition)\n       ↓ RouteReifier.doCreateRoute()\nEndpoint resolved from URI\n       ↓ ProcessorReifier.reifier(route, eipNode).addRoutes() [per output EIP]\n         ↓ makeProcessor() → createProcessor() [concrete EIP Processor]\n         ↓ wrapChannel() → DefaultChannel.initChannel()\n              [interceptors layered: InterceptStrategy wrapping in reverse order]\n              [advices added: tracer, debugger, message history, node history]\n         ↓ wrapChannelInErrorHandler() [ErrorHandler wraps channel output]\n         channel → route.getEventDrivenProcessors()\n       ↓ RoutePipeline(eventDrivenProcessors)\n       ↓ CamelInternalProcessor wrapping RoutePipeline [UoW, policies, JMX]\n       ↓ route.setProcessor(internal)\n       ↓ endpoint.createConsumer(processor) → Consumer holds full chain\n\nRUNTIME:\nConsumer.receives() → Exchange created\n  → CamelInternalProcessor [UoW begin, policy onExchangeBegin, JMX]\n    → RoutePipeline [PipelineTask iterates via ReactiveExecutor]\n      → DefaultChannel₁ [advices: trace/debug/history; error handler wraps]\n        → EIP Processor₁ (SetBody, Filter, etc.)\n      → DefaultChannel₂ [advices; error handler wraps]\n        → EIP Processor₂ (SendProcessor)\n          → ProducerCache → AsyncProducer.process()\n            → Endpoint₂.producer sends message\n  ← AsyncCallback chain unwinds back through Pipeline\n  ← CamelInternalProcessor [UoW complete, policy onExchangeDone, JMX]\nConsumer.releaseExchange()\n```\n\n### Interface Contracts Between Components\n\n- **Component → Endpoint**: `Component.createEndpoint(uri)` produces an `Endpoint`; the component owns URI parsing and endpoint configuration.\n- **Endpoint → Consumer**: `Endpoint.createConsumer(Processor)` injects the route's pipeline as the downstream handler; transport details stay encapsulated in the Consumer.\n- **Endpoint → Producer**: `Endpoint.createProducer()` produces a `Producer`; `SendProcessor` uses `ProducerCache` to pool and reuse producers.\n- **Channel contract**: `Channel.initChannel(route, definition, child, interceptors, nextProcessor, routeDef, first)` is called exactly once at build time; `postInitChannel()` finalizes JMX instrumentation after error handler is known.\n- **Pipeline contract**: `Pipeline` expects each step to be an `AsyncProcessor`; it manages continuations via `AsyncCallback.done(doneSync)` and `ReactiveExecutor.schedule()`.\n- **CamelInternalProcessorAdvice contract**: `before(exchange)` returns state object; `after(exchange, state)` receives it back; `hasState()` controls pooling behavior.\n\n---\n\n## Summary\n\nApache Camel routes a message by first translating the DSL model (`RouteDefinition` with its `ProcessorDefinition` tree) into a runtime graph at startup via `RouteReifier`: each EIP node becomes a concrete `Processor` wrapped in a `DefaultChannel` (which layers interceptors, tracing, debugging, and error handling via the AOP-style `CamelInternalProcessorAdvice` mechanism), and the ordered sequence of channels is collected into a `RoutePipeline`. The entire pipeline is then wrapped in a root `CamelInternalProcessor` that manages `UnitOfWork` and route-level cross-cutting concerns, and this processor is passed to `Endpoint.createConsumer()` so the transport-specific `Consumer` drives the pipeline when messages arrive. At runtime, messages flow as `Exchange` objects through `CamelInternalProcessor` → `RoutePipeline` → `DefaultChannel₁` → `EIPProcessor₁` → ... → `DefaultChannel_N` → `SendProcessor` → destination `Producer`, with asynchronous continuations scheduled by the `ReactiveExecutor` and each channel providing an interception boundary for error handling, management, and observability.\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
